<section class="md:mx-24 sm:mx-16">
<p>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/business/jan-marsalek-an-agent-for-russia-the-double-life-of-the-former-wirecard-executive-a-7e667c03-6690-41e6-92ad-583d94ba97e0" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Double Life of Former Wirecard Executive Jan Marsalek">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal lg:text-l md:text-base sm:text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Since the collapse of Wirecard, Jan Marsalek has been on the run and is one of the most wanted men in the world. A DER SPIEGEL investigation has revealed how he went underground and that he's a Russian spy.
</span>
</a>
</p>

<section class="md:mx-24 sm:mx-16">
<p>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/the-russian-invasion-a-visit-to-the-ukrainian-troops-in-the-trenches-on-the-front-a-b382bd59-8cbd-443c-9e7b-e1877d7e4a5b" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Horrors of Trench Warfare">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal lg:text-l md:text-base sm:text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Kyiv's soldiers have been fighting under the most difficult of conditions for two years. They are running out of ammunition and replacement troops are few. Many are no longer capable of imagining normal life. A visit to the front.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-s sm:text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Christoph Reuter
</span>
</a>
</p>

<section class="md:mx-24 sm:mx-16">
<p>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/the-marseille-experiment-macron-attempts-to-save-a-city-overtaken-by-drug-violence-a-bade2006-b7d7-433c-abf1-f053d56680aa" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Macron Attempts to Save a City Rocked by Drug Violence">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal lg:text-l md:text-base sm:text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Almost 50 people have recently died in drug-related violence in Marseille – even as ever more people are moving there. The government is investing billions in the city, but can it still be saved?
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-s sm:text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Britta Sandberg in Marseille, France
</span>
</a>
</p>
</section>

<section class="md:mx-24 sm:mx-16">
<p>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/everyday-repression-and-resignation-how-vladimir-putin-controls-the-russians-a-01a2ac3b-0d17-43ef-b0ce-a0b39c9e556a" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="How Vladimir Putin Controls the Russians">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal lg:text-l md:text-base sm:text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Russia has reverted to a dictatorship under President Vladimir Putin. Most people in the country seem to be accepting the war against Ukraine as well as the death of opposition activist Alexei Navalny. Why?
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-s sm:text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Benjamin Bidder, Ann-Dorit Boy und Christina Hebel in Hamburg and Moscow
</span>
</a>

<h2>

Indonesia's Brand New Capital
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl mb-12"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">A Mega-Project Raises Questions in Borneo</span></span>

<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/indonesias-brand-new-capital-a-mega-project-raises-questions-in-borneo-a-5da53568-cf27-4b24-ac79-39f77a72af6c" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="A Mega-Project Raises Questions in Borneo">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Indonesia is building a brand new capital city in the jungles of Borneo. Critics say it's a waste of money and will continue rampant environmental destruction. But might it perhaps become a model city one day?
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">

</span>
</a>

<section class="md:mx-24 sm:mx-16">
<p>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/right-wing-extremism-german-identitarians-are-trying-to-make-a-comeback-a-1fa09809-4097-4ab7-b397-7c29f3f9a33d" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="German Identitarians Are Trying to Make a Comeback">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal lg:text-l md:text-base sm:text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
The Identitarian Movement in Germany seemed to have ebbed. But now the right-wing extremists are making a comeback. They have close ties to the Alternative for Germany party and a notable financier who used to be an important member of the center-right Christian Democrats.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-s sm:text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Maik Baumgärtner, Ann-Katrin Müller, Sven Röbel und Wolf Wiedmann-Schmidt

<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/esther-horvath-photos-of-women-researchers-at-the-edge-of-the-earth-a-99ab502d-ac41-42e4-ac17-b61e06bc0908" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Photographing the Women of Svalbard">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Esther Horvath has for years been photographing women engaged in climate research in the Arctic. Her photos show the challenges they face as they go about their work in minus 30 degrees Celsius.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Jan Petter

<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/a-model-ignored-uncertain-future-for-successful-austrian-employment-program-a-0fde0a32-f7a3-4f04-9f65-368564b1a308" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Uncertain Future for Successful Austrian Employment Program">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

<header class="mb-12 lg:flex lg:justify-between lg:items-center md:flex md:justify-between md:items-center">
<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/trumps-threat-how-prepared-is-the-german-defense-industry-a-8666a348-8654-4626-9dca-9bdc4f4609e8" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="How Prepared Is the German Defense Industry">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Trump's Threat
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">How Prepared Is the German Defense Industry</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/trumps-threat-how-prepared-is-the-german-defense-industry-a-8666a348-8654-4626-9dca-9bdc4f4609e8" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="How Prepared Is the German Defense Industry">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Too little and too outdated: If the United States were to abandon its protection of Europe, the German arsenal of weapons would barely be enough to defend the country. Companies like Rheinmetall and Krauss-Maffei Wegmann are trying to change the status quo, but the industry is still too weak.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Matthias Gebauer, Martin Hesse und Gerald Traufetter
</span>
</a>
</section>

<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Good Morning Europe!
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Trump's NATO Comments Trigger Defense Debate in Europe</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/good-morning-europe-trumps-nato-comments-trigger-defense-debate-in-europe-a-3ea07d0c-d5cf-4d0a-9848-b69ba65978e0" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Trump's NATO Comments Trigger Defense Debate in Europe">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

</span>

<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
An Enemy of Russia and Europe
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Does Billionaire Arkady Volozh Really Belong on the EU Sanctions List?</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/does-russian-billionaire-arkady-volozh-really-belong-on-the-eu-sanctions-list-a-22c0af4b-a0a1-4323-bedf-b88d43be23c5" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Does Billionaire Arkady Volozh Really Belong on the EU Sanctions List?">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

Ammunition Shortages

<span class="inline-flex align-middle leading-none mr-4" data-contains-flags="Spplus-paid">

</span>
</span><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">German Chancellor Pledges To Boost Production for Ukraine</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/ammunition-shortages-german-chancellor-pledges-to-boost-production-for-ukraine-a-2b850f0b-b81d-4112-a52d-982cee1ea545" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="German Chancellor Pledges To Boost Production for Ukraine">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
With Europe falling significantly behind on its targets for ammunition production, German Chancellor Olaf Scholz is stepping in to help. He wants to significantly boost the domestic industry to assist in providing aid pledged to Ukraine.
</span>
</a>
</section>

<h2 class="w-full">

They Wanted Us To Be Happy.&#34;">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
An Israeli Hostage Discusses Her Time in Captivity
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">"Crying Was Forbidden. They Wanted Us To Be Happy."</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/hamas-hostage-chen-goldstein-almog-on-her-time-in-gaza-crying-was-forbidden-a-428c0acb-f56d-491f-8dcf-a3140d08b95d" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="&#34;Crying Was Forbidden. They Wanted Us To Be Happy.&#34;">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Hamas held Chen Goldstein-Almog and her children hostage for 51 days. In an interview, she talks about hunger, fear of death, conversations with her guards – and why she can't really be happy about being free again.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
A DER SPIEGEL Interview Conducted By Juliane von Mittelstaedt
</span>
</a>
</section>

<section>

<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

<header class="mb-12 lg:flex lg:justify-between lg:items-center md:flex md:justify-between md:items-center">
<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/can-the-german-people-stop-the-afds-far-right-rise-a-72fecc92-7da1-4a82-9ae9-f85111675462" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Can the German People Stop the AfD's Far-Right Rise?">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Over a Million at Protests
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Can the German People Stop the AfD's Far-Right Rise?</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/can-the-german-people-stop-the-afds-far-right-rise-a-72fecc92-7da1-4a82-9ae9-f85111675462" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Can the German People Stop the AfD's Far-Right Rise?">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Politicians in Germany have failed to find the means to successfully fight the rise of the far-right AfD. Now, hundreds of thousands of normal citizens have taken to the streets in efforts to stop the party. Although the protest movement includes broad swaths of society, it remains fragile.
</span>
</a>
</section>

"Reason of State"
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">The True Story Behind Merkel's Promise to Israel</span></span>
</span>

<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/reason-of-state-the-true-story-behind-merkels-promise-to-israel-a-00563b9e-0c66-4717-9331-e0bbb4cc8f88" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The True Story Behind Merkel's Promise to Israel">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

Former Israeli Prime Minister Ehud Olmert
</span>

Mine Clearing in Ukraine
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">"Dead Soldiers Lay Everywhere in the Fields, Ours and Russian"</span></span>

<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">

</span>

<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/a-model-for-europe-the-rise-of-post-fascists-in-northern-italy-a-de1dfee4-4811-4679-a363-83bd9c21e3df" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Rise of Post-Fascists in Northern Italy">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
A Model for Europe?
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">The Rise of Post-Fascists in Northern Italy</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/a-model-for-europe-the-rise-of-post-fascists-in-northern-italy-a-de1dfee4-4811-4679-a363-83bd9c21e3df" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Rise of Post-Fascists in Northern Italy">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
The centrist People's Party has ruled in South Tyrol since 1948. Now, though, the provincial governor is forming a coalition with the post-fascist party Fratelli d'Italia. Many are concerned that it could provide a blueprint for similar partnerships at the European level.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Walter Mayr in Bolzano, Italy
</span>
</a>
</section>

<header class="mb-12 lg:flex lg:justify-between lg:items-center md:flex md:justify-between md:items-center">
<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/assaults-harassment-and-beatings-does-the-eu-share-blame-for-police-violence-in-tunisia-a-1e6df924-7850-47a0-be2b-c10d03d7ec4c" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Does the EU Share Blame for Police Violence in Tunisia?">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Assaults, Harassment and Beatings
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Does the EU Share Blame for Police Violence in Tunisia?</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/assaults-harassment-and-beatings-does-the-eu-share-blame-for-police-violence-in-tunisia-a-1e6df924-7850-47a0-be2b-c10d03d7ec4c" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Does the EU Share Blame for Police Violence in Tunisia?">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
The West has provided the Tunisian security apparatus with millions of euros in funding. It had been earmarked for combating terror, curbing migration and strengthening the democratic transition. Instead, it has empowered the police, who now feel they are untouchable.
</span>
<span class="font-sansUI font-normal text-s text-shade-dark dark:text-shade-light" data-target-teaser-el="meta">
By Monika Bolliger in Tunis
</span>
</a>
</section>

"I'm Experimenting with Periodic Fasting"
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Interview with Weight Loss Drugs Inventor Lotte Bjerre Knudsen</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/business/interview-with-weight-loss-drugs-inventor-lotte-bjerre-knudsen-a-f2815950-ff24-4e87-b7e9-b6d6c1982d57" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Interview with Weight Loss Drugs Inventor Lotte Bjerre Knudsen">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Danish researcher Lotte Bjerre Knudsen is regarded as the inventor of the weight loss injections that made Novo Nordisk Europe’s most valuable and one of its most-hyped companies. In an interview, she discusses the revolution spawned by the drugs.
</span>

Interview conducted by Martin U. Müller und Alexander Preker in Copenhagen
</span>

<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/a-gaza-conundrum-the-story-behind-the-rise-of-hamas-a-d9e30bb6-2295-45a1-825c-dbd0c43c3613" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Story Behind the Rise of Hamas">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
A Gaza Conundrum
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">The Story Behind the Rise of Hamas</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/a-gaza-conundrum-the-story-behind-the-rise-of-hamas-a-d9e30bb6-2295-45a1-825c-dbd0c43c3613" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="The Story Behind the Rise of Hamas">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Even as all eyes were on the PLO, a small Islamist group slowly took root in the Gaza Strip in the late 1980s. But under the leadership of Yahya Sinwar, Hamas grew and grew, and ultimately became the murderous terror group it is today. This is its story.
</span>
</a>
</section>

<header class="mb-12 lg:flex lg:justify-between lg:items-center md:flex md:justify-between md:items-center">
<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/espionage-from-the-east-russia-is-a-storm-china-is-climate-change-a-7436be38-2088-4e10-b188-e5032ad0a367" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="&#34;Russia Is a Storm, China Is Climate Change&#34;">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Espionage from the East
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">"Russia Is a Storm, China Is Climate Change"</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/world/espionage-from-the-east-russia-is-a-storm-china-is-climate-change-a-7436be38-2088-4e10-b188-e5032ad0a367" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="&#34;Russia Is a Storm, China Is Climate Change&#34;">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Spying from China continues to grow in both volume and sophistication. The cyber-snoops from the People's Republic have moved beyond companies and are now seeking to exert influence on politics in Germany – all while keeping a close eye on dissidents and minorities.
</span>
</a>
</section>

<h2 class="w-full">
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/hamas-in-germany-arrests-suggest-terrorist-organization-is-operating-in-europe-a-ba8a9a89-b5bc-49a1-9247-3cbac9519a58" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Arrests Suggest Terrorist Organization Is Operating in Europe">
<span>
<span class="mb-4 block text-primary-base focus:text-primary-darker hover:text-primary-dark dark:text-shade-lightest dark:hover:opacity-moderate dark:hover:text-shade-lightest dark:focus:opacity-moderate dark:focus:text-shade-lightest font-sansUI font-normal lg:text-base md:text-base sm:text-s" data-target-teaser-el="topMark">
Hamas in Germany
</span>
</span>
<span class="block font-sansUI font-bold text-xl"><span class="hover:opacity-moderate focus:opacity-moderate"><span class="align-middle">Arrests Suggest Terrorist Organization Is Operating in Europe</span></span>
</span>
</a>
</h2>
</header>
<section>
<a href="https://www.spiegel.de/international/germany/hamas-in-germany-arrests-suggest-terrorist-organization-is-operating-in-europe-a-ba8a9a89-b5bc-49a1-9247-3cbac9519a58" target="_self" class="text-black dark:text-shade-lightest block" title="Arrests Suggest Terrorist Organization Is Operating in Europe">
<span class="font-serifUI font-normal text-base leading-loose mr-6" data-target-teaser-el="text">
Germany used to be considered a safe haven for Hamas, a place where the terror organization could raise money and build networks. Now, with the arrest of suspected members, fears are growing that Hamas could be planning attacks in Europe.
</span>
</a>
</section>
